. foreach n of local fe{  
  2.         dis "----------BREAK is `n'"
  3.         *Checking obs 
.         tabstat elevation2 if control_break_fe_400==`n' & sample==1, by(within_control) s(N) save
  4.         mat X1=r(Stat1) 
  5.         mat X2=r(Stat2) 
  6.         
.         if X1[1,1]!=. & X2[1,1]!=.{
  7.                 ttest elevation2 if control_break_fe_400==`n' & sample==1, by(within_control)
  8.                 
.                 if `r(p_l)'<=0.1{
  9.                         local felist `felist' `n'
 10.                         dis "`felist'"
 11.                 }
 12.         } 
 13. }
